### [236] [Beyond Runtime Enforcement: Shield Synthesis as Defensibility Analysis for Adversarial Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13621)
*Achraf Hsain,Sultan Almuhammadi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文论证了屏蔽式强化学习（shielded RL）的核心价值不在于作为运行时安全机制，而应作为设计时的分析工具。作者通过一个非对称的双人安全博弈框架，从形式化可防御性判决和可防御性指纹两个层面，为网络防御系统提供架构级的结构性洞察。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有屏蔽式强化学习被错误地定位为运行时安全机制，即通过自动机构造限制部署智能体的动作。作者认为这种定位忽略了同一套自动机理论工具在设计阶段的分析价值，因此提出将其重新解读为一种设计时的分析工具。

Method: 构建了一个非对称约束的双人安全博弈：防御方规范定义不安全区域，攻击方规范限制对手合法动作。通过吸引子计算和赢域提取求解博弈，获得可防御性判决。进一步，从吸引子结构提取拓扑级指标，与屏蔽约束下的多智能体对抗强化学习结合，构建"可防御性指纹"。

Result: 通过"What-if"分析发现：形式化可防御性与操作有效性衡量的是安全的不同维度——微小的架构变更可以显著改变操作结果，而形式化安全裕度几乎不变。屏蔽合成最有价值的产物是"可防御性判决"（系统能否被防御、在哪里被防御），而非安全的策略本身。

Conclusion: 屏蔽式强化学习的真正价值不在于作为部署安全智能体的运行时机制，而在于作为回答架构级问题的框架：系统是否可以被防御、在哪里可以被防御、以及如何被防御。可防御性判决才是最终输出，而非安全策略。

Abstract: Shielded reinforcement learning is typically presented as a runtime safety mechanism that compiles temporal-logic specifications into automata restricting an agent's actions. We argue this is the wrong product. The same automata-theoretic machinery -- specification compilation, product game construction, attractor computation, and winning-region extraction -- is better read as a design-time analytical instrument whose outputs are structural insights about a system rather than runtime constraints on a deployed agent.
  We instantiate this through a constrained two-player safety game for network defense. The two specifications are enforced asymmetrically: the defender specification defines the unsafe region of the game, whereas the attacker specification restricts the adversary's legal actions during attractor computation. Solving the game yields a defensibility verdict -- a formal certificate that a topology-specification pair is or is not defensible -- with the associated winning region and shield.
  Beyond the binary verdict, we derive topology-level metrics from the attractor structure and combine them with post-convergence behavior from shield-constrained adversarial multi-agent reinforcement learning. Together these form a defensibility fingerprint capturing both a network's formal safety properties and its operational behavior under adaptive play.
  A what-if analysis shows that formal defensibility and operational effectiveness capture distinct aspects of security: small architectural changes can produce large shifts in operational outcomes while leaving formal safety margins nearly unchanged. Shield synthesis is thus most valuable not as a deployment mechanism for safe agents, but as a framework for answering architectural questions about whether, where, and how a system can be defended. The defensibility verdict is the output, not the safe policy.

</details>

Abstract: Current LLM-based research agents have advanced through agent orchestration, yet largely overlook scientific knowledge orchestration. Existing works often reduce papers to abstracts, surface mentions, and flat \texttt{cites} edges, omitting key entities, claims, evidence, mechanisms, and method lineages essential for scientific reasoning. To this end, we introduce \textbf{Agents-K1}, an end-to-end knowledge orchestration pipeline that converts raw documents into agent-native scientific knowledge graphs. Agents-K1 integrates three components under a unifying theoretical foundation: a multimodal parser whose five-module schema captures entities, multimodal evidence, citations, and typed inter-entity relations across the full paper rather than abstracts alone; a 4B information-extraction backbone trained with GRPO under a rule-based reward; and a graphanything CLI, a tri-source agent interface that unifies web search, multimodal graph retrieval, and cross-document traversal. The same pipeline can be extended to general-domain corpora and to schema-conformant data synthesis. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Agents-K1 achieves superior performance in scientific information extraction, knowledge graph construction, and multi-hop scientific reasoning.

### [239] [Automated reproducibility assessments in the social and behavioral sciences using large language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13670)
*Tobias Holtdirk,Pietro Marcolongo,Anna Steinberg Schulten,Felix Henninger,Stefan Rose,Sarah Ball,Bolei Ma,Frauke Kreuter,Markus Weinmann,Stefan Feuerriegel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文展示了大型语言模型（LLMs）能够自动评估社会与行为科学研究的可重复性。基于76项已发表研究，LLM管道在41%的研究中恢复了原始效应量（Cohen's d ±0.05容忍度），并在96%的案例中得出与原始研究相同的定性结论，表现优于人类再分析（34%恢复率，74%定性一致率）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统可重复性评估依赖独立研究人员重新分析原始数据，这种人工方式资源密集且难以规模化。作者希望探索LLMs能否作为一种自动化、可扩展的替代方案来评估研究结果的可重复性。

Method: 使用N=76项来自行为与社会科学且有预定义主张的已发表研究，构建LLM管道生成效应量估计，并与原始研究发现及人类再分析结果进行比较。将LLM无法生成可行效应量的7项研究排除后，评估其余研究的效应量恢复率和定性结论一致性。

Result: LLM管道在41%的研究中恢复了原始效应量（Cohen's d ±0.05容忍度），在96%的案例中得出与原始研究相同的定性结论。相比之下，人类再分析人员的恢复率为34%，定性结论一致率为74%。

Conclusion: LLMs可以作为可重复性评估的可扩展工具，为系统审计社会与行为科学的实证结果提供基础。LLMs在定性结论一致性上显著优于人类，但在效应量精确恢复上与人类相当甚至略优。

Abstract: Reproducibility in the social and behavioral sciences is typically evaluated by independent researchers who reanalyze the original data to assess whether the published findings can be recovered. However, such approaches are resource-intensive and difficult to scale. Here, we show that large language models (LLMs) can automate reproducibility assessments. Using N=76 published studies with predefined claims from the behavioral and social sciences, we compare LLM-generated analysis with the original findings and human reanalysis. For 7 studies, the LLM could not produce a viable effect size estimate. For the remaining studies, our LLM pipeline recovered the original effect sizes in 41% of studies using a +/-0.05 tolerance in Cohen's d. Further, our LLM pipeline reached the same qualitative conclusion as the original study in 96% of cases, where conclusions indicate whether the reanalysis supports the original claim. For comparison, human reanalysts recovered the original effect sizes in 34% of studies and reached the same qualitative conclusion in 74% of cases. Together, these results show that LLMs can serve as a scalable tool for automated reproducibility assessment and provide a foundation for systematic auditing of empirical results in the social and behavioral sciences.

</details>

### [240] [Characterizing Tests in IoT Software: Practices, Challenges and Opportunities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12592)
*Rufeng Chen,Hengcheng Zhu,Wuqi Zhang,Zixu Zhou,Lili Wei*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文首次对开源物联网软件中的测试用例进行了实证研究，发现虽然测试数量不少但效果有限，主要挑战在于管理复杂的外部依赖交互，而模拟对象技术有望提升测试覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物联网软件缺陷可能导致严重后果（如智能门锁被非法入侵），但当前对物联网软件测试的实际情况知之甚少，缺乏系统性研究。

Method: 对开源物联网软件中的测试用例进行实证研究，评估测试用例的有效性，探索测试中面临的挑战，并分析模拟对象（mock objects）的使用情况。

Result: 物联网软件通常包含大量测试，但有效性有限；主要测试挑战是管理与其他网络依赖组件、文件系统、操作系统和数据库等外部依赖的复杂交互；模拟对象的使用与测试挑战高度相关。

Conclusion: 模拟对象与测试挑战的紧密对齐表明，模拟技术有潜力作为解决物联网软件测试复杂性和提升测试覆盖率的有效方案。

Abstract: The Internet of Things (IoT) is experiencing rapid growth. Smart devices are emerging in smart homes and industrial applications, performing mission-critical tasks. Bugs in IoT software can lead to severe consequences. For example, a buggy smart lock can allow unauthorized access to a private property. Testing is a primary practice to expose software bugs and ensure software quality. However, little is known about how IoT software is tested. To bridge this gap, we conducted the first empirical study on test cases in open-source IoT software. Specifically, we evaluated the effectiveness of test cases in IoT software, explored the challenges inherent in testing IoT software, and analyzed the usage of mock objects. Our results indicate that while IoT software often contains a considerable number of tests, their effectiveness remains limited. We identified the primary challenges in testing IoT software as managing complex interactions with various external dependencies, such as other network-reliant IoT components, file systems, operating systems, and databases. We also observed that the use of mock objects in IoT software closely aligns with our identified testing challenges. This alignment demonstrates the potential of mocking as a solution to enhance test coverage and address the complexities of IoT software testing.

</details>


### [241] [HybridCodeAuthorship: A Benchmark Dataset for Line-Level Code Authorship Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12620)
*Luke Patterson,Li Wang,Adam Faulkner*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了HybridCodeAuthorship基准，用于检测AI生成代码的混合创作问题。该基准包含Python代码文件，其中人类和AI编写的代码行交错出现，模拟真实使用AI代码助手的情况。实验表明这是一个具有挑战性的基准，最佳算法（AIGCode Detector）在块级和行级检测任务上F1得分分别为0.48和0.56。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI生成代码检测基准存在两个问题：一是主要基于学术性LeetCode风格的题目，二是假设代码片段完全是人类或AI创作的，无法反映实际工业代码库中AI与人类代码混合的现实情况。为了进行风险管理和生产力分析，需要细粒度的AI生成代码定位检测能力。

Method: 论文构建了HybridCodeAuthorship基准，利用CodeSearchNet收集GitHub开源仓库链接，构建了人类和AI代码行交错混合的Python代码文件数据集。然后使用两种最先进的AI生成代码检测算法在行级和块级两个粒度上进行性能评估。

Result: 最佳算法AIGCode Detector在块级检测任务上最高F1得分为0.48，在行级检测任务上最高F1得分为0.56，表明该基准具有较高挑战性。

Conclusion: HybridCodeAuthorship是一个更贴近真实工业场景的AI代码检测基准，现有算法性能有限，亟需更好的细粒度AI代码检测方法。

Abstract: Thanks to the rapid adoption of AI code assistants powered by large language models (LLMs), industry codebases are, increasingly, a hybrid of AI- and human-authored code. For risk management and productivity analysis purposes, it is crucial to enable fine-grained location detection of AI-generated code. To develop algorithms for this task, quality benchmarks are needed to assess performance. However, existing benchmarks tend to comprise academic, LeetCode-style problems and presume a code snippet is either completely human-authored or completely AI-authored, which is not reflective of the diverse intents and styles of industry codebases utilizing AI code assistants. To fill these gaps, we introduce HybridCodeAuthorship, a novel benchmark of Python code files with interleaved human- and AI-authored lines of code to simulate authentic utilization of AI code assistants. In this paper, we first present our dataset construction pipeline, which leverages CodeSearchNet, a massive collection of links to open sourced repositories on GitHub. We then benchmark the performance of two state-of-the-art AI-generated code detection algorithms at both the line- and chunk-level. Experimental results demonstrate that HybridCodeAuthorship is a challenging benchmark with a top-scoring algorithm, AIGCode Detector, obtaining a highest F1 score of 0.48 and 0.56 on chunk-level and line-level code detection tasks, respectively.

### [242] [Beyond Problem Solving: UOJ-Bench for Evaluating Code Generation, Hacking, and Repair in Competitive Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12864)
*Tingqiang Xu,Hangrui Zhou,Tianle Cai,Alex Gu,Kaifeng Lyu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出UOJ-Bench基准，评估LLM在编程教育场景中的代码生成、代码攻击和代码修复能力。发现最强模型一次性识别错误率不足50%，测试时扩展可提升至90%以上但计算成本高。前沿LLM能发现约5%满分提交中的隐藏错误，可作为在线评测系统的补充。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM在竞赛编程中表现出色，但其在辅助人类学习编程（特别是识别代码错误这一关键教育环节）方面的能力尚缺乏系统性评估。现有在线评测系统仅通过测试用例判断正误，难以发现隐藏的错误。

Method: 构建UOJ-Bench基准，包含三个任务：代码生成（根据问题描述编写代码）、代码攻击（找出他人代码中的错误）、代码修复（修正错误代码）。数据来自Universal Online Judge的真实用户提交，利用UOJ原生评测基础设施进行验证。

Result: 一次性评估下最强模型对已知错误提交的识别率不足50%。测试时扩展可将成功率提升至90%以上，但推理计算成本极高。最佳模型在约30道问题的满分提交中能发现超过5%的隐藏错误。

Conclusion: 前沿LLM已具备超越传统在线评测系统的潜力，能发现标准测试用例无法捕捉的代码错误，可作为编程教育中的辅助工具。但受限于计算成本，大规模部署仍需优化。

Abstract: Despite strong performance in competitive programming, the role of Large Language Models (LLMs) in supporting human learning in the same setting remains largely unexplored. In this work, we introduce UOJ-Bench, a benchmark designed to evaluate not only the problem-solving ability of LLMs, but also their ability to identify errors in human-written code -- a crucial educational activity traditionally supported by running test cases over online judge systems. UOJ-Bench consists of three distinct tasks: code generation, code hacking, and code repair, all constructed from real-world code submissions on the Universal Online Judge (UOJ) and evaluated through UOJ's native judging infrastructure. Our results show that under one-shot evaluation, even the strongest models fail to identify errors in more than 50% of a set of submissions that have been found to be incorrect by UOJ users. While test-time scaling improves success rates to above 90%, the substantial computational costs incurred from model inference limit its practicality for large-scale deployment. Despite these limitations, we find that the best-performing models under test-time scaling can uncover errors in over 5% of full-score submissions across roughly 30 problems, suggesting that frontier LLMs can already provide complementary signals beyond standard judging systems.

</details>


### [243] [The Rise of AI-Native Software Engineering: Implications for Practice, Education, and the Future Workforce](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12986)
*Mamdouh Alenezi*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了2016-2026年间48篇经过验证的同行评审文献，分析了GenAI、LLM和Agentic AI对软件工程的颠覆性影响。研究通过四Agent工作流程（文献发现、科学计量分析、课程转型和劳动力影响）进行，提出了AI原生软件工程的概念框架（意图、协作、验证）、九维能力模型、四阶段大学课程路线图、教师发展和劳动力转型策略，以及11个研究空白优先议程。证据显示生产力影响存在内部矛盾，强调了培养工程师判断力、验证和编排能力是AI原生时代核心挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GenAI、LLM和Agentic AI正在深刻重塑软件工程，但学术界对如何系统性地应对这一变革缺乏全面梳理。现有文献分散且结论矛盾，亟需一份系统性综述来整合证据、识别研究空白，并为教育、实践和劳动力提供指导框架。

Method: 采用四Agent研究工作流：文献发现、科学计量分析、课程转型、劳动力影响。从SE、ML、计算教育、人-AI协作和软件生产力等顶级会议/期刊中筛选出48篇经核实的同行评审文献（2016-2026），沿九个主题和三条轨迹（实践、教育、劳动力）进行综合。

Result: （1）发现2022年底后LLM-for-SE的年产出增长了约五倍；（2）证据在生产力影响的方向和程度上存在内部矛盾，收益强烈依赖于上下文；（3）提炼出AI原生SE的概念框架（意图、协作、验证）；（4）提出九维能力模型（规范、批判评估、Agent编排、元认知等）；（5）制定四阶段大学课程路线图及AI韧性评估方案；（6）提出11个优先研究空白。

Conclusion: AI原生时代的核心挑战不仅是代码生产，而是培养工程师的判断力、验证和编排能力。生产力影响高度依赖于上下文，需要教育体系进行系统性变革以培养适应新范式的软件工程师。

Abstract: Generative Artificial Intelligence (GenAI), Large Language Models (LLMs), and emerging Agentic AI constitute the most disruptive transformation in the history of software engineering (SE), reshaping development processes, required competencies, professional roles, and the educational outcomes that universities must deliver. This paper presents a systematic review of 48 verified, influential peer-reviewed publications (2016--2026) drawn from leading venues in software engineering, machine learning, computing education, human--AI collaboration, and software productivity. Studies were discovered, screened, and analyzed through a four-agent research workflow (Literature Discovery, Scientometric Analysis, Curriculum Transformation, and Workforce Impact) and were verified against primary sources. We synthesize the evidence along nine themes and three trajectories -- practice, education, and workforce -- and report a scientometric inflection in which annual LLM-for-SE output grew roughly five-fold after late 2022. From this synthesis we contribute: (i) a conceptual framework for AI-native software engineering organized around \emph{intent}, \emph{collaboration}, and \emph{verification}; (ii) a nine-dimension competency model spanning specification, critical evaluation, agent orchestration, and metacognition; (iii) a four-phase university curriculum roadmap with AI-resilient assessment; (iv) faculty-development and workforce-transformation strategies; and (v) a prioritized agenda of eleven research gaps. The evidence base is internally contradictory on the magnitude and direction of productivity effects, underscoring that benefits are strongly context-dependent and that educating engineers for judgment, verification, and orchestration -- rather than code production alone -- is the central challenge of the AI-native era.

### [244] [The End of Code Review: Coding Agents Supersede Human Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13175)
*Martin Monperrus*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文论证了基于LLM的编码代理已具备足够能力，可以完全替代传统人工代码审查，因为代理能以更低成本和更高吞吐量实现代码审查的所有目标，且人工审查在AI辅助开发中既无法提供有意义的保障，也无法扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战自1976年以来一直作为软件质量基石的人工代码审查流程，提出在编码代理能力达到新阈值后，传统人工审查不再是必要环节的观点。

Method: 通过两个核心论证展开：(1) 代码审查的每个既定目标都可被代理以更低成本和更高吞吐量实现；(2) 人类作为强制审查者的简单集成模式是死胡同，既不能提供有意义的保障，也无法随AI辅助吞吐量扩展。

Result: 提出编码代理已跨越能力阈值，能够完全替代传统人工代码审查的角色和功能。

Conclusion: 传统人工代码审查不再是软件质量管线的必要组成部分，需要重新设计AI时代下的软件开发质量保障流程。

Abstract: Code review has been the primary quality gate in software development since Fagan formalised code inspection in 1976. For five decades, having a human examine and comment on a colleague's changes before merge has been a cornerstone practice at organisations of every size. Coding agents are large language model (LLM)-based autonomous systems capable of reading, writing, testing, and repairing software. We argue that coding agents have crossed a threshold of capability at which traditional human code review is no longer a necessary component of a software quality pipeline. Our argument rests on two claims: every stated goal of code review can be served by agents at lower cost and higher throughput; the naive integration in which agents write code and humans remain the mandatory reviewers is a dead end because it neither provides meaningful assurance nor scales with AI-assisted throughput.

### [245] [ComAct: Reframing Professional Software Manipulation via COM-as-Action Paradigm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13239)
*Jiaxin Ai,Tao Hu,Xuemeng Yang,Shu Zou,Hairong Zhang,Daocheng Fu,Yu Yang,Hongbin Zhou,Nianchen Deng,Pinlong Cai,Zhongyuan Wang,Botian Shi,Kaipeng Zhang,Licheng Wen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出COM-as-Action范式，将专业软件交互从视觉控制重构为确定性程序合成，并构建了ComCADBench（首个工业CAD软件agent基准）和ComActor（通过三阶段框架训练的自纠正agent），实验证明该方法在长程任务中显著优于GUI-based方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算机使用agent存在根本局限：GUI-based agent受困于脆弱的视觉定位和长程误差累积，API-based方法则面临异构协议和不可访问的商业接口问题。

Method: 1. 识别Component Object Model (COM)作为统一的可执行抽象，提出COM-as-Action新范式；2. 构建ComCADBench首个工业CAD软件agent基准；3. 开发ComActor自纠正agent，通过渐进式三阶段框架训练；4. 构建ComForge平台，支持Windows容器中的大规模训练。

Result: 前沿闭源模型在GUI交互下成功率接近为零，COM-based执行带来显著提升；ComActor在ComCADBench上达到SOTA，在基线模型崩溃的长程任务中表现强鲁棒性，并能泛化到外部CAD基准。

Conclusion: COM-as-Action范式有效弥合了语法正确性与几何精度之间的差距，为专业工业软件自动化操作提供了新路径。

Abstract: Existing computer-use agents remain fundamentally limited in professional software manipulation: GUI-based agents suffer from fragile visual grounding and long-horizon error accumulation, while API-basedapproaches struggle with heterogeneous protocols and inaccessible commercial interfaces. In this work,we identify the Component Object Model (COM) as a unified executable abstraction, proposing COM-as-Action: a new paradigm that reframes professional software interaction as deterministic program synthesisrather than sequential visual control. To validate this paradigm in the most demanding environments, weintroduce ComCADBench, the first benchmark for agents operating real industrial CAD software. Ourexperiments reveal a substantial paradigm gap: frontier proprietary models achieve near-zero successunder GUI-based interaction, whereas COM-based execution yields substantial immediate gains. Tobridge the remaining gap between syntactic correctness and geometric accuracy, we develop ComActor, aself-correcting agent trained through a progressive three-stage framework, alongside ComForge, a scalableplatform for large-scale training in Windows containers. Extensive experiments show that ComActorachieves state-of-the-art performance on ComCADBench, with strong resilience in long-horizon taskswhere baselines collapse, and generalizes to external CAD benchmark.

### [246] [Mining Architectural Quality Under Agentic AI Adoption: A Causal Study of Java Repositories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13298)
*Oliver Aleksander Larsen,Mahyar T. Moghaddam*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 通过151个Java仓库（74个采用AI编码工具，77个匹配对照）的因果分析发现，AI工具采用后代码行数增长12.8%，但架构坏味总数未显著变化（+1.1%），导致密度下降6.7%仅为分母效应，并非架构质量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果研究仅关注代码层面（复杂度、静态分析警告），AI编码工具对软件架构层面的影响尚属未知，亟需因果证据。

Method: 收集151个开源Java仓库（74个有可检测的AI采用证据），经倾向得分匹配后，在13个月窗口内获取1,811个月度Arcan架构快照，采用交错DID和Borusyak插值估计量进行因果推断。

Result: AI工具采用后：坏味总数无显著变化（+1.1%, p=0.82），代码行数显著增长（+12.8%, p=0.003），导致架构坏味密度显著下降6.7%（p=0.004），但该下降完全是分母效应。多种稳健性检验支持这一结论。

Conclusion: AI编码工具并未改善架构质量，密度归一化指标在处理影响系统规模时会产生误导，因果挖掘研究应使用原始计数并明确分解效应来源。

Abstract: AI coding tools are now used by a majority of developers, and agentic use of these tools has popularized the practice colloquially called "vibe coding". Yet causal evidence on their effect on software architecture is scarce. Prior causal work has measured code-level outcomes (complexity, static analysis warnings); whether such degradation propagates to architecture-level outcomes remains unknown. We mine 151 open-source Java repositories, 74 with detectable agentic AI adoption (identified via configuration files and Co-Authored-By commit trailers) and 77 propensity-matched controls, across a 13-month per-repository window yielding 1,811 monthly Arcan snapshots. We estimate the causal effect of adoption on architectural smell density (ASD) with a staggered difference-in-differences design and the Borusyak imputation estimator, applying a causal design recently used for code-level metrics to the architecture level. Total smell counts are essentially unchanged (+1.1%, p = 0.82) while lines of code grow +12.8% (p = 0.003); the resulting 6.7% ASD decline (p = 0.004) is therefore a denominator effect rather than an architectural improvement. Per-type estimates and robustness checks (wild cluster bootstrap, Lee bounds, stale-observation sensitivity) corroborate the pattern; pre-trends are flat (Wald p = 0.90), consistent with parallel trends. Density-normalized outcomes can mislead when treatment affects system size: raw counts and explicit decomposition are required for causal mining studies of AI tool adoption. The complete replication package, including the curated 151-repository monthly panel, is publicly available.

</details>


### [247] [Toward Instructions-as-Code: Understanding the Impact of Instruction Files on Agentic Pull Requests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13449)
*Ali Arabat,Mohammed Sayagh*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文分析了15,549个AI生成的PR（来自AIDev数据集的148个项目），研究了指令文件（指导AI代理的文件）与AI代理性能之间的关系。结果表明，创建指令文件并不一定能带来更好的结果：约27.7%的项目合并率提升超过20%，但26.35%的项目反而下降。初步探索发现，成功提升合并率的项目通常拥有更长且结构更清晰的指令文件。研究呼吁将指令文件的开发视为软件工程活动（即"指令即代码"）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者为AI代理创建指令文件以指导其更高效地工作（如导航项目、定位组件、运行测试等），但目前缺乏对这些指令文件效果的系统性实证研究。论文旨在探究指令文件的创建与AI代理在PR生成中的表现（合并率、任务复杂度、合并所需努力）之间的关系。

Method: 基于AIDev数据集中的15,549个AI生成的PR（来自148个项目），从三个维度（合并率、代码变更量、合并努力）比较每个项目在创建指令文件前后的表现差异。

Result: 指令文件并不保证效果提升：27.7%的项目合并率提升≥20%，但26.35%的项目下降；代码变更量和合并努力方面也呈现类似的双向变化。初步探索发现，成功项目的指令文件更长且结构更清晰（更多章节和子章节）。

Conclusion: 指令文件的创建需要被视为一项软件工程活动（Instructions-as-Code），不能简单认为"有指令就更好"。需要进一步研究如何帮助 practitioners 更好地编写和结构化指令文件。

Abstract: AI-agents (e.g., GitHub Copilot) collaborate as teammates in different software engineering tasks, including code generation proposed through pull requests (Agentic-PRs). For better agent efficiency, developers create instruction files that guide the AI-agents, including how to navigate the project, locate the right components, run tests, respect best practices, and more. In this paper, we investigate the relationship between the creation of these instructions and the performance of AI-agents in creating better pull requests, which have a higher chance of success (i.e., the merge rate), address more complex tasks (e.g., code churn), and require less effort to be merged (e.g., time to merge). To this end, we analyze 15,549 agentic PRs from 148 projects in the AIDev dataset. Using the three dimensions, we compare each project before and after the creation of the instruction files. We find that specifying instructions for AI-agents does not necessarily lead to better results. With the instruction files, 27.7\% of the projects increased their merge rate by at least 20\%, while 26.35\% decreased it. The same observation is seen with the amount of changes (e.g., code churn, number of modified files) and with the efforts to merge an agentic PR (e.g., merge time and number of comments). From a first exploration, we find that projects that managed to increase their merge rate have substantially longer instruction files, which are also well structured into a higher number of sections and sub-sections. Our results motivate the need for research to assist practitioners in framing the development of instruction files as a software engineering activity (aka, \textbf{Instructions-as-Code}).

</details>


### [248] [Understanding the Rejection of Fixes Generated by Agentic Pull Requests -- Insights from the AIDev Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13468)
*Mahmoud Abujadallah,Ali Arabat,Mohammed Sayagh*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了AI编码代理（Copilot、Devin、Cursor、Claude）生成的拉取请求（PR）被拒绝的原因。发现46.41%的修复被拒绝，通过定性和定量分析识别出14个失败原因，归为四类：实现错误、CI流水线失败、代理无法执行、优先级低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编码代理生成的代码修复中有近半数被拒绝，造成大量人力资源和计算资源的浪费。理解这些失败模式对于更好地将AI代理整合为高效团队成员至关重要。

Method: 对AIDev数据集中306个未合并的PR进行代表性抽样，先进行定性研究识别拒绝原因，再进行定量分析验证。识别出14个原因，归纳为四大类。

Result: 发现14个拒绝原因分为四类：1) 实现错误（不完整、方法错误）；2) CI流水线失败（测试未通过）；3) 代理无法执行（未生成代码、会话丢失）；4) 优先级低。46.41%的PR被拒绝。

Conclusion: 需要从三个层面改进：1) 提示修复问题的正确方法；2) 明确不应采用的方法约束；3) 指导代理通过CI流水线验证实现且不引入破坏性变更。同时需要更好的任务优先级排序以减少资源浪费。

Abstract: AI coding agents are increasingly used to generate pull requests (PRs) that propose code fixes in software projects. From a first exploration of the AIDev dataset, we find that 46.41\% of the fixes proposed by the agents Copilot, Devin, Cursor, and Claude are rejected. This represents a significant amount of wasted resources that require human reviews, verifications, and running tests and validations for fixes that are merely discarded. Our goal in this paper is to understand the failure modes of AI-agents, an understanding that is crucial for better integrating AI-agents as efficient teammates. In this paper, we conduct a qualitative study on a representative sample of 306 non-merged pull requests created or co-authored by the agents mentioned earlier, followed by a quantitative analysis of the reasons for rejection. Our qualitative findings identify 14 reasons divided into four high-level categories for rejecting AI-agent fixes. We observe that developers can reject fixes due to fixes whose implementation is incorrect (e.g., incomplete, wrong approach), fixes that do not pass the continuous integration (CI) pipelines and fail tests, fixes for which the agent is unable to perform the implementation (e.g., no code generated, sessions lost), and fixes whose priority is low. Our results shed light on the importance of better guiding the model at these levels: (1) proposing hints about the approach to follow for fixing an issue, (2) outlining constraints or limitations regarding the approaches that should not be taken, and (3) instructing the agent on how to validate the implementation through CI pipelines and without introducing a breaking change. Our results suggest the need for good prioritization of tasks so that generated fixes do not lead to wasted human review efforts or wasted agent resources (e.g., tokens, compute, or allowed number of requests).

</details>

### [249] [Graph Reduction in Multirelational Networks: A Spreading-Oriented Reduction Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12581)
*Mateusz Stolarski,Michał Czuba,Piotr Bielak,Piotr Bródka*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出 SORB 框架，系统评估图缩减对影响力最大化任务的影响，发现缩减效果因网络类型和下游任务而异：单层网络中稀疏化保留种子质量，多层网络则导致排名退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实网络存在不完整、噪声和动态演化问题，大规模网络直接分析计算成本高。图缩减作为预处理步骤的作用及其对影响力最大化准确性的影响尚未被充分探索。

Method: 构建 SORB 基准框架，包含单层和多层真实网络，将图缩减（稀疏化/粗化）直接纳入评估流程，系统比较不同缩减策略对多个 IM 场景的影响。

Result: 缩减效果强烈依赖于网络类型和下游任务：单层网络上稀疏化保留种子质量；多层网络无论何种缩减策略均导致排名系统性退化。

Conclusion: 强调了在复杂网络传播研究中采用缩减感知、多任务评估的重要性。

Abstract: Real-world networks are inherently incomplete, noisy, and dynamically evolving, making it difficult to capture all actors and their relationships. Their scale often renders direct analysis computationally demanding. While influence maximisation (IM) has been widely studied, the role of graph reduction as a preprocessing step, and its impact on IM accuracy, remains underexplored. In this work, we introduce the Spreading-Oriented Reduction Benchmark (SORB), an open-source, standardised framework for systematically evaluating IM models across diverse task settings. SORB provides an extensible pipeline operating on a representative collection of real-world networks, including single- and multilayer structures, and accounts for graph reduction directly into the evaluation process. This design shifts the focus from analysing IM algorithms in isolation to quantifying how graph reduction alters predictive performance. Using SORB, we study the effects of sparsification and coarsening across multiple IM scenarios. Our results show that the impact of reduction is strongly dependent on both the network type (single-layer vs. multirelational) and the downstream task ($Gain@k$ vs. $\mathrm{AUC}_{\mathrm{cutoff}}$): sparsification preserves seed set quality on single-layer networks, whereas flattened multilayer networks exhibit systematic ranking degradation regardless of reduction strategy. These findings highlight the importance of reduction-aware, multi-task evaluation when studying spreading processes in complex networks.

</details>


### [250] [Orchestrating the Twin Transition in Multinational Corporations: Technology Roadmapping for Green and Digital Global Business Services](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12787)
*Han-Teng Liao,Karen Ang*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了全球商业服务（GBS）如何成为绿色与数字双重转型的“活实验室”，通过整合技术路线图（TRM）与国际电信联盟（ITU）的创新生态系统工具包，提出了一个社会技术框架。文献计量分析揭示了从流程自动化向“可持续智能”的演变，将GBS定位为连接宏观压力（如欧盟双重要求、碳边境调节机制）与AI原生工作流创新的“运营气闸”。研究还将这些集群映射到利益相关者参与画布上，指出波兰、葡萄牙和马来西亚等“中等强国”枢纽如何绕过中等收入陷阱，为全球价值链提供“第三条道路”。最终为领导者和创业支持网络提供了数据驱动的设计方法，丰富了工业5.0的理论理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨国企业在全球业务中面临双重压力：既要实现数字化转型提升效率，又要满足日益严格的环保要求（如欧盟的绿色双重要求和碳边境调节机制）。在此背景下，GBS作为“活实验室”为探索绿色与数字双重转型提供了独特视角，但目前缺乏系统的社会技术框架来指导这一转型过程。

Method: 本研究采用混合方法：1) 将技术路线图（TRM）与ITU ICT创新生态系统工具包进行理论综合；2) 对研究集群进行文献计量分析，揭示演变趋势；3) 将分析结果映射到利益相关者参与画布上，识别关键枢纽节点。

Result: 研究发现：1) GBS正从基础流程自动化向“可持续智能”方向演进；2) GBS单元扮演了连接宏观政策压力与微观创新（AI原生工作流）的“运营气闸”角色；3) 波兰、葡萄牙、马来西亚等“中等强国”枢纽正在绕过中等收入陷阱，在地缘政治分裂的背景下为全球价值链提供“第三条道路”。

Conclusion: 本文为领导者和创业支持网络提供了数据驱动的设计方法，用于协调人才和供应链流动，从而丰富了工业5.0的概念理解，并确立了GBS作为在动荡、多极化的数字经济中导航的主要机制。

Abstract: Global Business Services (GBS) have emerged as a "living laboratory" for the Twin Transition of Green and Digital Transformation, as multinational corporations (MNCs) face increasing pressure to harmonize digital efficiency with environmental stewardship. Aiming to derive a socio-technical framework, this paper synthesizes Technology Roadmapping (TRM) with the International Telecommunication Union (ITU) ICT-centric innovation ecosystem toolkit. A bibliometric analysis of research clusters reveals an evolutionary shift from basic process automation toward "Sustainable Intelligence," identifying the GBS unit as a central "operational airlock" that mediates between landscape pressures -- such as the EU's dual mandate and Carbon Border Adjustment Mechanisms -- and niche innovations in AI-native workflows. The study further maps these clusters onto a stakeholder engagement canvas, highlighting how resilient "Middle Power" hubs in Poland, Portugal, and Malaysia are bypassing the middle-income trap to provide a "third way" for global value chains amidst a bifurcated geopolitical cloud. The results offer a data-driven design approach for leaders and entrepreneurial support networks to orchestrate talent and supply chain flows, thereby enriching the conceptual understanding of Industry 5.0 and the role of GBS as a primary mechanism for navigating a volatile, multipolar digital economy.

</details>


### [251] [To Share or Not to Share: Orchestrating Trustworthy Data in Global Value Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12788)
*Han-Teng Liao,Chang-Yi Kao*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出基于国际数据空间（IDSA）框架的RegTech参考架构，用于解决欧盟碳边境调节机制（CBAM）下半导体-石化产业链的数据主权与监管透明度矛盾，以台北-槟城走廊为例，结合数字产品护照（DPP）、Agentic AI和绿色金融，构建可持续的全球价值链。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欧盟CBAM即将实施，全球半导体价值链面临监管透明度与数据主权之间的结构性紧张关系，现有技术框架无法有效协调强制性的CBAM要求、自愿性的SBTi框架以及SSbD框架之间的复杂叠加关系。

Method: 采用IDSA框架构建RegTech参考架构，区分CBAM强制要求与SBTi自愿框架；引入前瞻性路线图方法，将上游物理脆弱性转化为循环负反馈回路；通过主权数据交换赋能数字产品护照（DPP）；集成Agentic AI实现自主合规。

Result: 聚焦台北-佩南技术走廊，详述了主权数据交换如何驱动DPP进而推动全球商业服务（GBS）能力需求；提供了Agentic AI自主合规与FinTech绿色融资的整合方案。

Conclusion: 该架构为全球工业集群实现主权化、可持续和透明的价值链提供了一个可扩展的蓝图。

Abstract: As the EU Carbon Border Adjustment Mechanism (CBAM) approaches, the global semiconductor value chain faces growing structural tensions between regulatory transparency and data sovereignty. This article proposes a RegTech reference architecture using the International Data Spaces (IDSA) framework to orchestrate trustworthy environmental telemetry across the semiconductor-petrochemical nexus. The framework distinguishes the mandatory CBAM requirements from voluntary Science Based Targets initiative (SBTi) frameworks, while addressing the additive complexities of the Safe-and-Sustainable-by-Design (SSbD) framework. Moving beyond standard linear technology stacks, we introduce a prospective roadmapping methodology that transforms upstream physical vulnerabilities into circular, negative feedback loops. Focusing on the Taipei and Penang technology corridor, the article details how sovereign data exchange enables Digital Product Passports (DPPs) to drive Global Business Services (GBSs) capability demands. Finally, we discuss the integration of Agentic AI for autonomous compliance and FinTech green financing, providing a scalable blueprint for global industrial clusters to achieve sovereign, sustainable, and transparent value chains.

### [252] [MIDSim: Simulating Multi-Channel Information Diffusion in Social Media with LLM-Powered Multi-Agent System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13140)
*Lexi Liu,Qi Cao,Yuanhao Liu,Huawei Shen,Xueqi Cheng*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 提出了一个基于LLM的多智能体系统，用于模拟多通道信息扩散，同时考虑社交传播和算法推荐，在三个真实社交媒体数据集上优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有信息扩散研究主要关注社交链接传播，忽视了平台算法（如推荐系统）带来的其他扩散渠道，也无法捕捉用户行为复杂性。

Method: 提出了LLM驱动的多智能体系统，用大语言模型实例化个性化用户代理，联合建模社交暴露流和算法推荐流两种传播通道。

Result: 在微博、小红书、Twitter三个真实扩散事件数据集上，框架能够真实模拟宏观扩散现象并生成多样化的评论内容，显著优于基线方法。

Conclusion: LLM多智能体系统能够有效模拟多通道信息扩散，弥补了传统模型忽视算法推荐通道和用户行为复杂性的缺陷。

Abstract: Information diffusion in social media shapes public opinion and collective behavior, making its modeling and simulation an important research problem. Existing studies have investigated information diffusion through epidemic-based, cascade-based, and point process models. However, they predominantly focus on diffusion through social links, overlooking other diffusion channels enabled by platform algorithms (e.g., recommender systems) and failing to capture user behavioral complexity. To address these limitations, we propose an LLM-powered multi-agent system for simulating multi-channel information diffusion, where large language models instantiate personalized user agents and the diffusion process jointly models social and algorithmic exposure streams. We further construct three real-world diffusion dataset spanning Sina Weibo, RedNote, and Twitter, containing diffusion records, user profiles, historical posts, and social relationships. Experimental results on real diffusion events show that our proposed framework realistically simulate macro diffusion phenomenon and generate diverse comment content, significantly outperforming baselines.

</details>
